                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     Entrance to alien base at Rocca Pia, Italy discovered as two aliens met with Italians, UFO Sighting News.
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3013040743805417765" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                      <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       Meet Kenio. Through some analysys on the photo it was established that this "fellow" is over 2.4 meter tall...
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       oh, I forgot...he is an alien of the W56 group, also known as Akrij.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GoVPxpm5Q8o/TdSakgI84UI/AAAAAAAAA10/89P-a9j4HIQ/s1600/Kenio%252C+W56.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                         <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-GoVPxpm5Q8o/TdSakgI84UI/AAAAAAAAA10/89P-a9j4HIQ/s400/Kenio%252C+W56.jpg" width="420"/>
                        </span>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-C4DAp9t3WK8/UCRj-BiTPwI/AAAAAAAAFuM/qGwahtrIj9I/s1600/W56,+CTR,+alien,+aliens,+base,+rocca+pia,+italy,+friends,+friendship,+Akrij,+UFO,+UFOs,+sighting,+sightingsScreen+Shot+2012-08-10+at+9.24.42+AM.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                         <img border="0" height="302" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-C4DAp9t3WK8/UCRj-BiTPwI/AAAAAAAAFuM/qGwahtrIj9I/s400/W56,+CTR,+alien,+aliens,+base,+rocca+pia,+italy,+friends,+friendship,+Akrij,+UFO,+UFOs,+sighting,+sightingsScreen+Shot+2012-08-10+at+9.24.42+AM.png" width="400"/>
                        </span>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       Entrance to alien base at Rocca Pia, Italy discovered as two aliens met with Italians, UFO Sighting News. Aliens give message of HOPE, FRIENDSHIP and LOVE.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <center>
                       <a href="http://scottcwaring.files.wordpress.com/2011/05/60af88c0-710b-4d4e-b928-98c757d93dc3113.jpg">
                        <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                         <img border="0" height="308" src="http://scottcwaring.files.wordpress.com/2011/05/60af88c0-710b-4d4e-b928-98c757d93dc3113.jpg" style="margin: 5px;" width="400"/>
                        </span>
                       </a>
                      </center>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                       It had been kept secret for half a century, but only just recently came to light after the death of one the men involved (Bruno Sammaciccia had asked for it to be kept secret until after his death).
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <center>
                       <a href="http://scottcwaring.files.wordpress.com/2011/05/533dc164-1f10-4fa5-bfb6-8dce37aa75a2114.jpg">
                        <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                         <img border="0" height="310" src="http://scottcwaring.files.wordpress.com/2011/05/533dc164-1f10-4fa5-bfb6-8dce37aa75a2114.jpg" style="margin: 5px;" width="400"/>
                        </span>
                       </a>
                      </center>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                       In Pescara, during the 50s to 70s, a group of extraterrestrials had contacted a number of unsuspecting people directly. This project was called 'Amicizia.' These men would be brought to their (etheric) 'bases' located on earth and apparently on board the UFOs.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                       The people involved were of high social and cultural status, among them was the notable Console Alberto Perego. This is a collection of testimonials from them, which also shows excellent quality footage and photography of the phenomena, as well as apparent 'messages' (of love and goodwill) given to us from these beings.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       ------------
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       This may just be coincidence, but Robert "Bob" Lazar, a scientist who worked on a flying saucer in Area S4 had once stated that the USAF gave him reading info about aliens and in the documents it stated there was 56 space faring species of aliens known. That could explain why the aliens in Italy called themselves W56. Howeverthe meaning of the W has continued to elude me.(Scott C. Waring)
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                       <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="315" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/FZn3ewgAHFk?rel=0" width="560">
                       </iframe>
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span class="" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       The story of Friendship -or simply the story, as we always called it- is a true one. It involved a group of Italian and non-Italian people for many years, between 1956 and 1990. Some of these people, including myself, are still alive. We had direct, face-to-face meetings with the Friends (also called W56), who are extraterrestrials coming both from planets in our own Galaxy (at a distance of one hundred thousand light years) and from other Galaxies. Here on the Earth they reached the maximum number of two hundred, living inside underground and undersea bases, some of them along the Adriatic coast, at a depth of about 20 km/12 miles. The first, historical base was located under the area of Ascoli Piceno, a small town in central Italy.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span class="" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       The Friends are our elder brothers. They are human. Indeed, in comparison its we terrestrials who are less than human. They are much more human than we are, and that is why they do not show themselves. They are too human For us it is easy to flatter them, but envying them is even easier, due to their perfect humaneness
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                       The Friends are not the only extraterrestrials who have come to the Earth. Individuals from various other populations are among us, because the Earth is a very particular planet inside the economy of this part of the Universe. The aim of the Friends presence is not to study us (they know us quite well, better than we do ourselves!), but to help us. In fact, the Friends are unhappy about the very high level of hate, violence and injustice on the Earth, and about the anti-humanistic trend of our science and technology. Being able to see our thoughts and feelings, the Friends see what we hide behind our masks, words and smiles
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div>
                       <span class="A;" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div>
                        <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                         Compared with all the other populations visiting the Earth, the Friends have a quite peculiar and precious characteristic to offer us: they have a very special and close connection with the subtle levels that regulate the destiny of the Earth and with what they call the Soul of the Universe, beyond the physical or phenomenal level. Thus, the Friends have a sort of general control over everything that occurs, but they are only allowed to intervene under particular conditions. Everything happens as in an extremely elaborate chess game, with rules that I cannot even touch upon here.
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <div>
                        <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                         <br/>
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                        UREDDA -in one of the Friends languages- is the energy that is produced by the Love between people, particularly between the Friends and our group, following a pact between them and us and the many events that brought us together.
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <div>
                        <span class=";" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: large;">
                         UREDDA is a kind of energy, but the Friends are not the worshippers of Energy, as other populations are. The Friends follow Love, which is also the source of good energies such as UREDDA, but is itself beyond any energy.
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <div>
                        <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bbDSLkoMwTg/VTETAx4lqXI/AAAAAAAAbZE/1bwJBNww0Y8/s1600/iphone%2C%2Bw56%2C%2Bpizza%2C%2Bimac%2C%2Bsteve%2Bjobs%2C%2BMJ12%2C%2BET%2C%2Bai%2C%2Bapp%2C%2BRome%2C%2BDARPA%2C%2Bipad%2C%2BClinton%2C%2BPresident%2C%2Bitouch%2C%2Biwatch%2C%2Bgame%2C%2Bgames%2C%2BBlizzard%2C%2Bstone%2C%2Bjewel%2C%2Bgem%2C%2Bfree%2C%2Bapple%2C%2Bnews%2C%2Bgoogle%2C%2Btech%2C%2Bgizmodo%2C%2Bcute%2C%2BWikileaks%2C%2BJustin%2BBieber%2C%2BSelena%2BGomez%2C%2B.png" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                          <img border="0" height="172" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bbDSLkoMwTg/VTETAx4lqXI/AAAAAAAAbZE/1bwJBNww0Y8/s1600/iphone%2C%2Bw56%2C%2Bpizza%2C%2Bimac%2C%2Bsteve%2Bjobs%2C%2BMJ12%2C%2BET%2C%2Bai%2C%2Bapp%2C%2BRome%2C%2BDARPA%2C%2Bipad%2C%2BClinton%2C%2BPresident%2C%2Bitouch%2C%2Biwatch%2C%2Bgame%2C%2Bgames%2C%2BBlizzard%2C%2Bstone%2C%2Bjewel%2C%2Bgem%2C%2Bfree%2C%2Bapple%2C%2Bnews%2C%2Bgoogle%2C%2Btech%2C%2Bgizmodo%2C%2Bcute%2C%2BWikileaks%2C%2BJustin%2BBieber%2C%2BSelena%2BGomez%2C%2B.png" width="640"/>
                         </a>
                        </div>

        if (entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
          for (var k in entry.gd$extendedProperty) {
            if (entry.gd$extendedProperty[k].name == 'blogger.contentRemoved') {
              return '&lt;span class="deleted-comment"&gt;' + entry.content.$t + '&lt;/span&gt;';
            }
          }

        return entry.content.$t;
      }

        cursor = null;
        var comments = [];

            var comment = {};
            // comment ID, parsed out of the original id format
            var id = /blog-(\d+).post-(\d+)/.exec(entry.id.$t);
            comment.id = id ? id[2] : null;
            comment.body = bodyFromEntry(entry);
            comment.timestamp = Date.parse(entry.published.$t) + '';
            if (entry.author &amp;&amp; entry.author.constructor === Array) {
              var auth = entry.author[0];
              if (auth) {

                  name: (auth.name ? auth.name.$t : undefined),
                  profileUrl: (auth.uri ? auth.uri.$t : undefined),
                  avatarUrl: (auth.gd$image ? auth.gd$image.src : undefined)
                };

            }

              if (entry.link[2]) {
                comment.link = comment.permalink = entry.link[2].href;
              }
              if (entry.link[3]) {
                var pid = /.*comments\/default\/(\d+)\?.*/.exec(entry.link[3].href);
                if (pid &amp;&amp; pid[1]) {

                }

                }
              }
            }

I don't want to influence you in any negative way as you can and will decide for yourself truth from non truth. Every atom of everything around us is light..... yes its all light dense and cold some of it may be,.... but yes light! We live in a holographic Universe....... If you could see what scientists have discovered about matter cooled down to absolute Zero that is -459.67 Fahrenheit which is absolute Zero, you would be truly enlightened. A single grain of sand, silica in nature starts revealing the truth about our Universe, Its holographic! Under the microscope we see not one grain of sand but a cloud of the same object! Why you say? Well because it has been cooled down so much it starts to lose its memory of where it is in space and time, It has no weight, can be multiplied up to 300 times or more, the number really doesn't matter and if you try removing one of the objects from the cloud ((it)) vanishes out of existence! Its called ((Bose Einstein Condensate)). My brother in-law who is a World renowned Physicist, has discussed this fact with me and we both agree once you can wrap your head around it everything and I mean everything starts opening up for you..... The fact we are not alone ,.... That fact you me everybody and everything is one consciousness.... We are riding on the back of a Titan! Its just in this lifetime whether we can come to this realisation before our time comes. We are more, so much more than most can, for now imagine. In this physical form we have the illusion of separateness. But you me everybody are at different stages of the path to enlightenment. We are all treading the same path,... but we get too tied up in the necessities of our everyday lives. So every thing around us is a wonder because it shouldn't exist by all intense and purposes.

                            <p class="comment-content" id="bc_0_27MC">
                             The W stands for Double Victory. From Stefano Breccia's Mass Contact:
                             <br/>
                             <br/>
                             "56 of course stands for the year when this history began; the 'W' stands for 'double victory' (in Italian, the letter 'W' is named 'Double V'; moreover, the Italian word 'vittoria' means 'victory'; therefore W = V + V = Victory + Victory). 'When you win your enemies  they were telling us  you have still to gain another victory, this time against yourselves, against your pride.' Their true name was 'Akrij' (The English pronunciation should be something like 'Aukree')."
                             <br/>
                             <br/>
                             Breccia, Stefano (2009-02-04). Mass Contacts (Kindle Locations 3950-3953). AuthorHouse. Kindle Edition.
                            </p>

                   "Heres to the crazy ones, the misfits, the rebels, the troublemakers, the round pegs in the square holes the ones who see things differently  theyre not fond of rules You can quote them, disagree with them, glorify or vilify them, but the only thing you cant do is ignore them because they change things they push the human race forward, and while some may see them as the crazy ones, we see genius, because the ones who are crazy enough to think that they can change the world, are the ones who do."

                <h2 class="title">
                 About This Site &amp; Me.
                </h2>
                <div class="widget-content">
                 <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; margin-left: 0px;   font-family:Georgia, serif;font-size:medium;">
                  <span id="yui_3_2_0_14_131355092788487" style="font-family:Arial;">
                   Hi, my name is Scott C. Waring and I wrote a few books and am currently a ESL School Owner in Taiwan. I have had my own UFO sighting up close and personal, but that's how it works right? A non believer becomes a believer when they experience their first sighting. You witnessed it, your perceptual field changes, so now you need to share it.
                   <o:p id="yui_3_2_0_14_131355092788497">
                   </o:p>
                  </span>
                 </p>

                   <br/>
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; margin-left: 0px;   font-family:Georgia, serif;font-size:medium;">
                  <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family:Arial;">
                   I created this site to help the UFO community get a little bit organized. I noticed that there was a lot of chaos when searching for UFO sighting reports, so I hope this site helps. I wanted to support those eyewitnesses who have tried to tell others about what they have seen, yet were laughed at by even closest of friends.
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt; margin-left: 0px;   font-family:Georgia, serif;font-size:medium;">

                  <span id="yui_3_2_0_14_1313550927884181" style="font-family:Arial;">

They have a trickle down theory in hopes of slowly getting citizens use to the idea that we are not alone in universe and never have been. The truth is being leaked drop by drop until one day we look around and find ourselves neck high in it.
                  </span>
                 </p>

                  <span id="yui_3_2_0_14_131355092788494" style="font-family:Arial;">

        var myPostContent = new RegExp('post-footer');
        var elem = this.getElementsByTagName('div');

        var url;
        var title = "";
        
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; elem.length; i++)
        {
            var classes = elem[i].className;
            if (myclass.test(classes))
            {   
            	var container = elem[i];
            	url = window.location.href;
            	
                for (var b = 0; b &lt; container.childNodes.length; b++)
                {
                    var item = container.childNodes[b].className;
                    if (myTitleContainer.test(item))
                    {
                        var link = container.childNodes[b].getElementsByTagName('a');
                        if (typeof(link[0]) != 'undefined')
                        {
                            var url = link[0].href;
                            var title = link[0].innerHTML;
                        }

                    var doubleq = new RegExp('"', 'g');

                    title = title.replace(doubleq, '&#34;', 'gi');

        }
    return true;
